# PokemonHackStudio Planning And Progress

## Current Focus

`PHS-T79` is complete as a policy/proof-first binary mutation safety row: direct ROM byte editing, repoint apply, free-space allocation apply, checksum repair, export, emulator launch, and binary writes remain blocked until a later implementation row adds explicit guarded writers.

`PHS-T112G` is complete: Gen V `files/a` archive-group roots now surface a shallow manual-only `nitroArchiveGroupInventory` summary row through NDS catalog, CLI JSON, `resource-index`, and app Resources while preserving detailed `files/a/**` child rows; Gen V editors, raw source writes, extraction/decompression, NARC packing, build/playtest execution, ROM export, mutation apply, and binary writes remain disabled.

`PHS-T112F` is complete: Gen V `data/` roots now surface a shallow manual-only `dataInventory` summary row through NDS catalog, CLI JSON, `resource-index`, and app Resources while preserving detailed `data/encounters/*` preview rows; Gen V editors, raw source writes, extraction/decompression, NARC packing, build/playtest execution, ROM export, mutation apply, and binary writes remain disabled.

`PHS-T112E` is complete: Gen V source/config roots now surface manual-only summaries for `Makefile`, `config.mk`, optional linker configs, shallow `src`/`asm`/`include` inventory, and Black/White/B2/W2 marker folders while retaining preview-only readiness, source-role, and action-state facts; Gen V editors, raw source writes, extraction/decompression, build/playtest execution, NARC packing, ROM export, mutation apply, and binary writes remain disabled.

`PHS-T57I` is complete: Ruby/Sapphire local `src/data/battle_moves.c` `gBattleMoves` rows now draft, preview, apply, back up, and reload through the existing Moves flow while move identity/constants, descriptions, contest data, TM/HM/tutor compatibility, generated/reference rows, ROM writes, and broad schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only.

`PHS-T57J` is complete: Ruby/Sapphire local `src/data/pokedex_entries_en.h` `gPokedexEntries` rows and `src/data/pokedex_text_en.h` Pokedex text declarations now draft, preview, explicitly apply, back up, and reload through the existing Species flow while TM/HM, egg, tutor, assets, generated/reference rows, ROM writes, national dex identity changes, missing row insertion, and broad schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only; evolution rows are covered by `PHS-T57K` and level-up rows by `PHS-T57L`.

`PHS-T57K` is complete: Ruby/Sapphire local `src/data/pokemon/evolution.h` `gEvolutionTable` rows now draft, preview, explicitly apply, back up, and reload through the existing Species flow while missing evolution row insertion, TM/HM, egg, tutor, assets, generated/reference rows, ROM writes, and broad schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only; level-up rows are covered by `PHS-T57L`.

`PHS-T57L` is complete: Ruby/Sapphire local `src/data/pokemon/level_up_learnsets.h` `g*LevelUpLearnset` blocks now draft, preview, explicitly apply, back up, and reload through the existing Species flow while egg moves, tutor moves, assets, missing learnset block insertion, symbol renames, constants/identity changes, generated/reference rows, ROM writes, and broad schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only; TM/HM rows are covered by `PHS-T57M`.

`PHS-T57M` is complete: Ruby/Sapphire local `src/data/pokemon/tmhm_learnsets.h` `gTMHMLearnsets` rows now draft, preview, explicitly apply, back up, and reload through the existing Species flow while egg, tutor, assets, generated/reference rows, ROM writes, non-local source rows, and broad schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only.

`PHS-T57N` is complete: Ruby/Sapphire local `src/data/trainers_en.h` `gTrainers` rows and `src/data/trainer_parties.h` party blocks now draft, preview, explicitly apply, back up, and reload through the existing Trainers flow while trainer constants/identity changes, unsupported party source shapes, generated/reference rows, ROM writes, trainer assets, row insertion/removal/reorder, and broad schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only.

`PHS-T98T` is complete: Platinum direct-child `res/trainers/classes/*.json` rows now expose existing top-level scalar trainer-class fields through the existing NDS semantic mutation gate while nested trainer-class directories, `res/trainers/resources/**`, non-JSON rows, generated/reference/container rows, ROM/export/rebuild/playtest paths, nested edits, row insertion, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only.

`PHS-T98S` is complete: Platinum direct-child `res/field/matrices/*.json` rows now expose existing top-level scalar matrix fields through the existing NDS semantic mutation gate while nested matrix directories, `res/field/maps/**`, `res/field/area_data/**`, map binaries, map tables, scripts/text, generated/reference/container rows, ROM/export/rebuild/playtest paths, nested edits, row insertion, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only.

No implementation row is currently active. `PHS-T98R` is complete: Diamond/Pearl `arm9/src/trainer_data.c` `sTrainerClassGenderCountTbl[]` rows now expose integer trainer class gender-count scalars through the existing NDS semantic mutation gate while non-integer expressions, row add/remove/reorder, other trainer C anchors, binary trainer rows, NARC/container rows, generated/reference rows, ROM/export/rebuild paths, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T78F` is complete: local source-backed Expansion `s*LevelUpLearnset` blocks in `src/data/pokemon/level_up_learnsets.h` and `src/data/pokemon/level_up_learnsets/*.h` now edit through the existing Species draft -> mutation preview -> explicit apply path while missing block insertion, symbol renames, generated `all_learnables.json`, generated outputs, reference rows, ROM writes, constants/identity, TM/HM/tutor/egg/evolution/Pokedex/assets/forms, and broad Expansion schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T98Q` is complete: Diamond/Pearl `files/fielddata/eventdata/*.json` rows now expose top-level scalar field-event fields through the existing NDS semantic mutation gate while nested event arrays/objects, nested event directories, map matrices/tables, `arm9` map/script C anchors, non-JSON rows, NARC/container rows, generated/reference rows, ROM/export/rebuild paths, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T98P` is complete: HeartGold/SoulSilver `files/fielddata/eventdata/zone_event/*.json` rows now expose top-level scalar zone-event fields through the existing NDS semantic mutation gate while nested event arrays/objects, nested zone-event directories, binary script rows, map matrices, NARC/container rows, generated/reference rows, ROM/export/rebuild paths, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T98O` is complete: Platinum `res/field/events/*.json` rows now expose top-level scalar field-event fields through the existing NDS semantic mutation gate while nested event arrays/objects, nested event directories, matrices, map binaries, scripts, generated/reference/container rows, ROM/export/rebuild work, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T78E` is complete: local source-backed Expansion `src/data/text/move_descriptions.h` declarations now edit through the existing move draft -> mutation preview -> explicit apply path while constants, contest data, TM/HM/tutor compatibility, generated outputs, reference rows, ROM writes, and broad Expansion move schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T57F3` is complete: source-backed Pokemon front/back profile sprite imports now require 64x64 PNGs with a 16-color palette limit, preserve provenance and PNG metadata, stage through the existing Species draft -> mutation preview -> explicit apply path, back up source PNGs before replacement, and keep generated conversion outputs, binary palettes, ROM writes, and bulk package import blocked. `PHS-T98N` is complete: Platinum `res/battle/moves/*.json` rows now expose top-level scalar move fields through the existing NDS semantic mutation gate while nested move values, nested move directories, non-JSON move rows, NARC/container rows, generated/reference rows, ROM/export/rebuild work, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T116` is complete: app-owned workspace saves/autosaves/discards and patch export artifact roots now share symlink-aware containment, patch export backups use collision-resistant roots, project-switch dirty guards account for all current drafts, Items selection stays aligned through hidden filters, Encounters first-open loads live source rows, Graphics exposes only source-backed mutation controls, and the first shared loader/facade seams are split out of `WorkbenchStore` while existing mutation-plan gates stay intact. `PHS-T112D` is complete: Gen V NDS catalog, CLI JSON, `resource-index`, and app Resources rows now share a `Gen V Action State` fact that keeps editing/apply, build, playtest, and export actions disabled while source inventory stays preview-only. `PHS-T57D` is complete: local `.pokeemeraldExpansion` `src/data/pokemon/species_info.h` `gSpeciesInfo` scalar row fields now draft, preview, explicitly apply, back up, and reload through the existing Species flow while type/ability/egg-group composites, learnsets, evolutions, Pokedex rows/text, assets, forms, config/generated/family supplement/reference rows, ROM writes, and broad Expansion schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T57H` is complete: Ruby/Sapphire local `src/data/pokemon/base_stats.h` `gBaseStats` rows now draft, preview, apply, back up, and reload through the existing Species flow while learnsets, evolutions, Pokedex, assets, cries/forms, generated/reference rows, ROM writes, and broad schema rewrites remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T98M` is complete: Diamond/Pearl `files/itemtool/itemdata/**/*.json` rows now expose top-level scalar item fields through the existing NDS semantic mutation gate while nested item arrays/objects, binary item rows, C anchors outside the existing item mapping row, NARC/container rows, generated/reference rows, ROM/export/rebuild work, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only. `PHS-T98L`, `PHS-T98K`, `PHS-T98J`, and `PHS-T78D` are complete with their prior write postures intact, and `make validate-nds` now includes the Diamond/Pearl trainer class gender C-anchor, Diamond/Pearl field-event JSON, HGSS zone-event JSON, Platinum field-event JSON, Platinum/HGSS/DP encounter, Diamond/Pearl item JSON, and Platinum move JSON semantic CLI plan/apply tests. `PHS-T114`, `PHS-T98I`, and `PHS-T78C` remain complete with their prior write postures intact; broader BW/BW2 readiness remains the `PHS-T112` Candidate umbrella. `PHS-T115` is complete: the code-review remediation batch stabilized source-tree write containment, blocked patch export side effects, NDS semantic parsing, app async/store cleanup, metadata-only asset bundling, CLI blocked-result exits, and validation proof while preserving the existing writer gates.

- `PHS-T95` adds read-only Gen IV map/script/text readiness relationships to NDS data catalogs and Resources: map, matrix, script, text, filesystem manifest, and container rows now expose preview-only status, related-row counts/domains, and explicit blocked actions for external editors, compilers, extraction, rebuild, NARC packing, and ROM export.
- `PHS-T94` adds read-only NDS graphics/container preview metadata on top of `PHS-T100` fingerprints: sampled Nitro members can surface ready preview hints, while compressed, unsupported, too-short, and unreadable members are explicitly blocked without extraction, decompression, conversion, rebuild, mutation apply, ROM export, or materialized preview files.
- `PHS-T96` adds the first semantic Gen IV editor layer on top of `PHS-T91`: eligible Platinum source-backed JSON rows expose editable top-level scalar fields in Resources and CLI semantic plan/apply commands, while still lowering to the existing NDS data mutation plan so source hashes, size checks, backups, explicit apply, and blocked ROM/NARC/reference/generated policies remain unchanged.
- `PHS-T97` adds read-only Gen IV text bank previews: NDS text records now carry preview status, decoded string counts, decoded sample strings, blocked writer/export actions, CLI JSON, and Resources facts for safe source text, JSON message banks, and BMG-like rows without adding semantic mutation eligibility, extraction, rebuild, ROM export, or binary/container writes.
- `PHS-T98A` expands that semantic layer to Platinum trainer data JSON rows under `res/trainers/data`, exposing scalar fields such as name, class, and double-battle flags while nested party/items/messages and trainer resource/class JSON stay outside semantic editing.
- `PHS-T98B` expands that semantic layer to eligible Platinum item JSON rows under `res/items`, exposing top-level scalar fields such as name, price, and field-use flags while nested effect arrays and CSV item indexes stay outside semantic editing.
- `PHS-T98C` expands that semantic layer to existing Platinum species JSON evolution tuples, exposing method/parameter/target fields such as `evolutions.0.parameter` while preserving the current source-backed mutation-plan gate; evolution add/remove/reorder, HGSS/DP, PMD-Sky, container/generated/reference rows, ROMs, extraction, rebuilds, emulator launch, ROM export, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only.
- `PHS-T98D` expands the semantic layer to HeartGold/SoulSilver personal JSON rows under `files/poketool/personal`, exposing source-backed scalar fields such as `species` through the same NDS mutation-plan gate; HGSS trainer/item rows, Diamond/Pearl C anchors, NARC/generated/reference rows, ROMs, extraction, rebuilds, emulator launch, ROM export, and binary writes remain blocked/read-only.
- `PHS-T99` adds read-only NDS migration planning metadata: ROM-backed NARC rows, source-tree NARCs, unpacked archive directories, and NitroFS manifests now report possible source-tree and extracted-directory targets, unsupported preservation/rebuild steps, blocked actions, CLI JSON, and source/ROM Resources facts without extracting, repacking, rebuilding, exporting, or writing ROM/container/source outputs.
- `PHS-T100` adds bounded read-only member fingerprints to NDS NARC and unpacked archive summaries: sampled members expose path/index, size, extension, leading magic, conservative format/compression hints, confidence, facts, and CLI JSON so future graphics, text, map, and migration rows can route opaque members without extraction, decompression, rebuilds, mutation apply, or ROM/container writes.
- `PHS-T101` hardens the semantic edit planner against repeated field inputs: duplicate keys now return `NDS_DATA_SEMANTIC_FIELD_DUPLICATE`, keep the original draft text, and lower to a blocked plan with no applyable changes.
- `PHS-T82` adds a preview-only playtest debugging plan: core and CLI now report mGBA debugger/GDB/Lua/access-log commands, planned debug artifacts, and optional BizHawk/VBA-M capability rows; the app Playtest tab renders the same plan while keeping debug launch, emulator embedding, ROM mutation, and artifact writes disabled.
- `PHS-T75` completes the next asset-writer hardening wave: source asset provenance/validation now covers PNG and source `.pal` inputs, binary `.gbapal` bytes are blocked from source `.pal` replacement, Pokemon species asset imports keep their existing mutation-plan gate, and trainer front/palette replacement is limited to existing explicit source-backed PNG/`.pal` files resolved from `trainerPic` references. Shared trainer-pic constants warn because multiple trainers can be affected, but remain applyable after preview.
- `PHS-T57F` closes the first Pokemon asset compatibility slice after the broader species/trainer import activation: source-backed footprint PNG imports preserve provenance and detected PNG metadata, require 16x16 two-color footprint sources, surface palette/format diagnostics in core and app provenance UI, and continue to apply only through the existing species mutation-plan gate with hash/size freshness checks and backups. Icon and profile-specific sprite lanes remain split to `PHS-T57F2`.
- `PHS-T84` adds native `.inc` command argument editing: core and CLI plan/apply exactly one existing map-local argument, preserve indentation/command/comments, explicitly block shared/project-wide `.inc`, generated/unsupported `.inc`, Poryscript-generated `.inc`, labels/directives/whole-body replacement, and keep source writes behind backups plus source hash/size freshness checks.
- `PHS-T76` is closed as the Poryscript safety detection slice for `PHS-T84`: `.pory` discovery, `#line` provenance, poryswitch and preprocessor facts, generated `.inc` relationship reporting, and blocked apply diagnostics are implemented without invoking compilers or copying Poryscript behavior.
- `PHS-T77` turns the map workflow plans into writers where the destination is safe: visual export writes ignored artifacts under `.pokemonhackstudio/exports/maps`, while map duplication apply checks stale snapshots and destination conflicts, writes new map/layout source atomically, backs up modified map/layout index files, and returns the duplicated map ID for selection/reload by app surfaces.
- Dev-loop timing captured during `PHS-T36`: warm direct `map-visual` CLI smokes remained fast (`pokeemerald` `MAP_PETALBURG_CITY` in 0.15s; `pokefirered` `MAP_BATTLE_COLOSSEUM_2P` in 0.12s), while `make validate` took 37.84s and `make verify` took 17.71s with the Xcode bundle phase still copying 2 local source projects every build. `PHS-T39` later replaced that recopy with an unchanged-bundle reuse path.

- `PHS-T14` finished the Build/Patch/Playtest preview workflow: `patch-manifest` accepts `--base-rom`, reports selected base ROM path/SHA1/size/candidate match, distinguishes base ROM mismatch, and the app now has a Patch tab with safe patch/base ROM selectors, project/resource base ROM options, manifest/dry-run/diagnostic rows, playtest artifact rows, and Copy Report JSON while keeping apply/export/build/run disabled.
- `PHS-T13` hardened the read-only table parser: descriptors can carry known-field metadata and opt into unknown-field warnings; table parsing now reports missing/unterminated initializers and unsupported bracketed entries with spans; field extraction only reports top-level designators so nested trainer party and TM/HM members do not become false unknown fields; and SourceIndex rows surface the diagnostics while preserving raw source bodies.
- Reference refresh added pinned source-first refs for `pokeemerald`, `pokefirered`, and `agbcc`; `docs/reference-improvement-audit.md` now captures the comparison against current code and the prioritized follow-up rows.
- Reference corpus centralization moved PokemonHackStudio's 30-repo reference bench into `/Users/bryan/projects/reference-repos`, tagged the central index/profiles with `ref.family.pokemonhackstudio`, and converted ignored `references/*` bench paths into compatibility aliases while leaving active working decomps and local ROM inputs in place.
